---

### 19.2 渲染性能优化

**面试问题：如何进行前端渲染性能优化？**

**参考答案：**

**一、渲染性能基础**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      浏览器渲染流程                              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  HTML Parser ──> DOM Tree ──> Style ──> Layout ──> Paint        │
│                                           │                     │
│                                           ▼                     │
│                                     Composite                   │
│                                           │                     │
│                                           ▼                     │
│                                     Display                     │
│                                                                 │
│  优化策略：                                                    │
│  1. 减少Layout（重排）                                          │
│  2. 减少Paint（重绘）                                           │
│  3. 减少Composite（合成）                                        │
│  4. 使用GPU加速                                                 │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、避免不必要的重排和重绘**

```typescript
// 1. 使用transform和opacity进行动画
// 避免（触发重排）
element.style.width = '100px';
element.style.height = '100px';
element.style.margin = '10px';

// 推荐（只触发合成）
element.style.transform = 'translateX(100px)';
element.style.opacity = '0.5';
element.style.scale = '1.2';

// 2. 使用CSS类批量修改样式
// 避免
element.style.width = '100px';
element.style.height = '100px';
element.style.color = 'red';

// 推荐 - 切换类名
element.classList.add('active');

// CSS
.active {
  width: 100px;
  height: 100px;
  color: red;
}

// 3. 缓存布局属性
// 避免 - 每次读取都触发重排
const width = element.offsetWidth;
const height = element.offsetHeight;
element.style.width = width + 10 + 'px';

// 推荐 - 缓存后再修改
const width = element.offsetWidth;
const height = element.offsetHeight;
requestAnimationFrame(() => {
  element.style.width = width + 10 + 'px';
});

// 4. 使用文档片段
// 避免 - 多次操作DOM
const list = document.getElementById('list');
items.forEach(item => {
  const li = document.createElement('li');
  li.textContent = item.text;
  list.appendChild(li);
});

// 推荐 - 使用文档片段
const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
items.forEach(item => {
  const li = document.createElement('li');
  li.textContent = item.text;
  fragment.appendChild(li);
});
list.appendChild(fragment);
```

**三、React渲染优化**

```typescript
// 1. 使用React.memo优化组件
const UserCard = React.memo(({ user }) => {
  return (
    <div className="user-card">
      <img src={user.avatar} alt={user.name} />
      <h3>{user.name}</h3>
    </div>
  );
}, (prevProps, nextProps) => {
  // 自定义比较逻辑
  return prevProps.user.id === nextProps.user.id;
});

// 2. 使用useMemo缓存计算结果
function UserList({ users, filter }) {
  const filteredUsers = useMemo(() => {
    return users.filter(user =>
      user.name.toLowerCase().includes(filter.toLowerCase())
    );
  }, [users, filter]);

  return filteredUsers.map(user => (
    <UserCard key={user.id} user={user} />
  ));
}

// 3. 使用useCallback缓存回调
function Parent() {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

  const handleItemClick = useCallback((id) => {
    console.log('Clicked:', id);
  }, []);

  return <List items={items} onItemClick={handleItemClick} />;
}

// 4. 列表渲染优化
function UserList({ users }) {
  return (
    <ul>
      {users.map(user => (
        <UserItem
          key={user.id} // 使用唯一ID，不要用index
          user={user}
        />
      ))}
    </ul>
  );
}

// 5. 使用虚拟列表
import { FixedSizeList } from 'react-window';

function VirtualList({ items }) {
  const, style }) => Row = ({ index (
    <div style={style}>
      {items[index].name}
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <FixedSizeList
      height={500}
      itemCount={items.length}
      itemSize={50}
      width="100%"
    >
      {Row}
    </FixedSizeList>
  );
}
```

**四、Vue渲染优化**

```typescript
// 1. 使用v-show和v-if
// v-if: 条件不渲染，切换时有销毁/创建开销
<template v-if="show">
  <HeavyComponent />
</template>

// v-show: 始终渲染，只是切换display
<template v-show="show">
  <HeavyComponent />
</template>

// 2. 使用computed
computed: {
  filteredItems() {
    return this.items.filter(item =>
      item.name.includes(this.search)
    );
  }
}

// 3. 使用v-for的key
// 避免 - 使用index
<div v-for="(item, index) in items" :key="index">

// 推荐 - 使用唯一ID
<div v-for="item in items" :key="item.id">

// 4. 使用Object.freeze冻结不需响应式的对象
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      // 大列表数据不需要响应式
      bigList: Object.freeze(largeArray)
    };
  }
};

// 5. 使用虚拟滚动
import VueVirtualScroller from 'vue-virtual-scroller';

<RecycleScroller
  :items="largeArray"
  :item-size="50"
  key-field="id"
>
  <template #default="{ item }">
    <div>{{ item.name }}</div>
  </template>
</RecycleScroller>
```

**五、减少DOM操作**

```typescript
// 1. 批量DOM操作
// 避免
for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
  const div = document.createElement('div');
  div.textContent = i;
  document.body.appendChild(div);
}

// 推荐 - 批量创建后一次性插入
const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();
for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
  const div = document.createElement('div');
  div.textContent = i;
  fragment.appendChild(div);
}
document.body.appendChild(fragment);

// 2. 使用innerHTML时注意性能
// 避免 - 多次innerHTML
element.innerHTML = '<div>A</div>';
element.innerHTML = '<div>B</div>';

// 推荐 - 构建字符串后一次性赋值
let html = '';
for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
  html += `<div>${i}</div>`;
}
element.innerHTML = html;

// 3. 使用DocumentFragment
function createList(items) {
  const fragment = document.createDocumentFragment();

  items.forEach(item => {
    const li = document.createElement('li');
    li.textContent = item.name;
    fragment.appendChild(li);
  });

  return fragment;
}

list.appendChild(createList(items));
```

**六、事件优化**

```typescript
// 1. 事件委托
// 避免 - 为每个子元素绑定事件
listItems.forEach(item => {
  item.addEventListener('click', handleClick);
});

// 推荐 - 事件委托到父元素
list.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
  const target = event.target.closest('li');
  if (target) {
    handleClick(target.dataset.id);
  }
});

// 2. 防抖和节流
// 防抖 - 等待停止后执行
function debounce(fn, delay) {
  let timer;
  return function(...args) {
    clearTimeout(timer);
    timer = setTimeout(() => fn.apply(this, args), delay);
  };
}

// 节流 - 固定间隔执行
function throttle(fn, interval) {
  let lastTime = 0;
  return function(...args) {
    const now = Date.now();
    if (now - lastTime >= interval) {
      lastTime = now;
      fn.apply(this, args);
    }
  };
}

// 使用
const handleScroll = throttle(() => {
  console.log('Scroll:', window.scrollY);
}, 200);

window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll);

// 3. requestAnimationFrame
function animate() {
  // 使用RAF优化动画
  element.style.transform = `translateX(${position}px)`;
  requestAnimationFrame(animate);
}
```

**七、内存优化**

```typescript
// 1. 清理定时器
function Component() {
  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      // 定时任务
    }, 1000);

    // 清理函数
    return () => clearInterval(timer);
  }, []);
}

// 2. 清理事件监听
function Component() {
  useEffect(() => {
    const handleResize = () => {
      // 处理resize
    };

    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
    };
  }, []);
}

// 3. 避免内存泄漏
// 常见原因：
// - 全局变量
// - 未清理的定时器
// - 未取消的事件监听
// - 闭包引用
// - 分离的DOM引用

// 解决方案
class Component {
  private observer: IntersectionObserver | null = null;

  componentDidMount() {
    this.observer = new IntersectionObserver(() => {});
  }

  componentWillUnmount() {
    // 清理观察者
    if (this.observer) {
      this.observer.disconnect();
      this.observer = null;
    }
  }
}
```

---

### 19.3 内存泄漏排查与解决

**面试问题：如何排查和解决JavaScript内存泄漏问题？**

**参考答案：**

**一、内存泄漏概述**

内存泄漏是指程序在申请内存后，无法释放已申请的内存空间，导致内存占用持续增长，最终可能导致应用崩溃。

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      内存泄漏类型                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  1. 全局变量泄漏                                                │
│     function leak() {                                          │
│       variable = 'some large data';  // 未声明的全局变量       │
│     }                                                          │
│                                                                 │
│  2. 闭包泄漏                                                    │
│     function outer() {                                         │
│       const largeData = new Array(1000000).fill('x');          │
│       return function inner() {                                │
│         console.log(largeData);  // 闭包引用                   │
│       };                                                       │
│     }                                                          │
│                                                                 │
│  3. DOM引用泄漏                                                 │
│     const elements = [];                                       │
│     function addElement() {                                   │
│       const div = document.createElement('div');               │
│       elements.push(div);  // 数组引用                        │
│     }                                                          │
│                                                                 │
│  4. 定时器泄漏                                                  │
│     setInterval(() => {                                        │
│       // 持续运行                                               │
│     }, 1000);  // 未清理                                        │
│                                                                 │
│  5. 事件监听泄漏                                                │
│     element.addEventListener('click', handler);  // 未移除   │
│                                                                 │
│  6. Map/Set和WeakMap/WeakSet使用不当                           │
│     const cache = new Map();                                   │
│     cache.set(element, data);  // 引用导致无法GC               │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、内存泄漏排查工具**

```typescript
// 1. Chrome DevTools - Memory面板
// 使用步骤：
// 1. 打开Chrome DevTools
// 2. 选择Memory面板
// 3. 选择堆快照类型
// 4. 记录初始状态
// 5. 执行操作
// 6. 再次记录状态
// 7. 对比快照

// 2. Performance Monitor
// 实时监控内存使用
function performanceMonitor() {
  setInterval(() => {
    const memory = performance.memory;
    console.log({
      jsHeapSize: memory.jsHeapSizeLimit,
      totalJSHeapSize: memory.totalJSHeapSize,
      usedJSHeapSize: memory.usedJSHeapSize
    });
  }, 1000);
}

// 3. 内存泄漏检测工具
class MemoryLeakDetector {
  private snapshots: any[] = [];
  private observer: PerformanceObserver | null = null;

  // 开始监控
  start() {
    if (typeof performance !== 'undefined' && 'memory' in performance) {
      this.observer = new PerformanceObserver((list) => {
        for (const entry of list.getEntries()) {
          console.log('Memory usage:', entry);
        }
      });
      this.observer.observe({ entryTypes: ['measure', 'navigation'] });
    }
  }

  // 记录快照
  takeSnapshot(label: string) {
    if (window.gc) {
      window.gc(); // 强制垃圾回收
    }

    const memory = (performance as any).memory;
    this.snapshots.push({
      label,
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      usedJSHeapSize: memory.usedJSHeapSize,
      totalJSHeapSize: memory.totalJSHeapSize
    });
  }

  // 分析泄漏
  analyze() {
    if (this.snapshots.length < 2) {
      console.log('Need more snapshots');
      return;
    }

    const first = this.snapshots[0];
    const last = this.snapshots[this.snapshots.length - 1];

    const growth = last.usedJSHeapSize - first.usedJSHeapSize;
    const growthPercent = (growth / first.usedJSHeapSize) * 100;

    console.log('Memory Growth:', {
      bytes: growth,
      percent: growthPercent.toFixed(2) + '%'
    });

    if (growthPercent > 10) {
      console.warn('Possible memory leak detected!');
    }
  }
}
```

**三、常见内存泄漏场景与解决方案**

```typescript
// 1. 全局变量泄漏
// 问题代码
function leak1() {
  variable = 'large data'; // 隐式全局变量
}

function leak2() {
  this.variable = 'large data'; // this指向全局对象
}

// 解决方案
'use strict';
function fixed1() {
  let variable = 'large data'; // 声明变量
}

// 2. 闭包泄漏
function leak() {
  const largeData = new Array(1000000).fill('x');

  return function() {
    console.log(largeData[0]); // 闭包引用largeData
  };
}

// 解决方案 - 手动释放
function fixed() {
  const largeData = new Array(1000000).fill('x');

  const handler = function() {
    console.log(largeData[0]);
  };

  // 不需要时手动释放
  handler.clearData = function() {
    largeData.length = 0;
  };

  return handler;
}

// 3. DOM引用泄漏
const elements = [];
function addElement() {
  const div = document.createElement('div');
  elements.push(div);
}

function removeElement(index) {
  // 只是从数组移除，但DOM还在内存中
  elements.splice(index, 1);
}

// 解决方案 - 正确清理
function removeElementFixed(index) {
  const element = elements[index];
  if (element && element.parentNode) {
    element.parentNode.removeChild(element);
  }
  elements.splice(index, 1);
}

// 4. 定时器泄漏
class Component {
  private timer: NodeJS.Timeout | null = null;

  start() {
    this.timer = setInterval(() => {
      this.process();
    }, 1000);
  }

  // 解决方案 - 组件卸载时清理
  componentWillUnmount() {
    if (this.timer) {
      clearInterval(this.timer);
      this.timer = null;
    }
  }
}

// 5. 事件监听泄漏
class Component {
  private boundHandler: (e: Event) => void;

  constructor() {
    this.boundHandler = this.handleClick.bind(this);
    window.addEventListener('resize', this.boundHandler);
  }

  // 解决方案 - 移除事件监听
  componentWillUnmount() {
    window.removeEventListener('resize', this.boundHandler);
  }
}

// 6. Map/Set泄漏
const cache = new Map();
function addToCache(key, value) {
  // 问题：key是对DOM元素的强引用
  cache.set(key, value);
}

// 解决方案 - 使用WeakMap
const weakCache = new WeakMap();
function addToCacheFixed(key, value) {
  // WeakMap允许垃圾回收
  weakCache.set(key, value);
}
```

**四、React内存泄漏处理**

```typescript
// 1. useEffect清理
function UserProfile({ userId }) {
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;

    fetchUser(userId).then(user => {
      if (!cancelled) {
        setUser(user);
      }
    });

    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
    };
  }, [userId]);

  return <div>{user?.name}</div>;
}

// 2. useRef存储可取消的值
function SearchResults({ query }) {
  const abortControllerRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    // 取消之前的请求
    if (abortControllerRef.current) {
      abortControllerRef.current.abort();
    }

    abortControllerRef.current = new AbortController();

    fetchResults(query, { signal: abortControllerRef.current.signal })
      .then(results => setResults(results))
      .catch(error => {
        if (error.name !== 'AbortError') {
          console.error(error);
        }
      });

    return () => {
      abortControllerRef.current?.abort();
    };
  }, [query]);

  return <ul>{results.map(r => <li key={r.id}>{r.name}</li>)}</ul>;
}

// 3. 自定义Hooks防泄漏
function useInterval(callback, delay) {
  const savedCallback = useRef(callback);

  useEffect(() => {
    savedCallback.current = callback;
  }, [callback]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (delay !== null) {
      const id = setInterval(() => savedCallback.current(), delay);
      return () => clearInterval(id);
    }
  }, [delay]);
}

function useEventListener(eventName, handler, element = window) {
  const savedHandler = useRef(handler);

  useEffect(() => {
    savedHandler.current = handler;
  }, [handler]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const eventListener = (event) => savedHandler.current(event);
    element.addEventListener(eventName, eventListener);

    return () => {
      element.removeEventListener(eventName, eventListener);
    };
  }, [eventName, element]);
}

// 4. 清理订阅
function ChatRoom({ roomId }) {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const unsubscribe = subscribeToRoom(roomId, (message) => {
      setMessages(prev => [...prev, message]);
    });

    return () => {
      unsubscribe(); // 取消订阅
    };
  }, [roomId]);

  return <MessageList messages={messages} />;
}
```

**五、Vue内存泄漏处理**

```typescript
// 1. 组件销毁清理
export default {
  data() {
    return {
      timer: null,
      observer: null,
      events: []
    };
  },

  mounted() {
    // 定时器
    this.timer = setInterval(this.process, 1000);

    // 观察者
    this.observer = new IntersectionObserver(this.handleIntersect);
    this.observer.observe(this.$refs.target);

    // 事件
    window.addEventListener('resize', this.handleResize);
  },

  beforeDestroy() {
    // 清理定时器
    if (this.timer) {
      clearInterval(this.timer);
      this.timer = null;
    }

    // 清理观察者
    if (this.observer) {
      this.observer.disconnect();
      this.observer = null;
    }

    // 移除事件监听
    window.removeEventListener('resize', this.handleResize);
  },

  methods: {
    handleIntersect(entries) {},
    handleResize() {}
  }
};

// 2. 指令清理
Vue.directive('clickoutside', {
  bind(el, binding) {
    el.__clickoutside__ = (event) => {
      if (!(el === event.target || el.contains(event.target))) {
        binding.value(event);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener('click', el.__clickoutside__);
  },

  unbind(el) {
    document.removeEventListener('click', el.__clickoutside__);
    delete el.__clickoutside__;
  }
});
```

**六、内存泄漏预防最佳实践**

```typescript
// 1. 严格模式
'use strict';

// 2. 使用const和let
// 避免var，防止变量提升导致的意外全局变量

// 3. 及时清理
class ResourceManager {
  private resources: Resource[] = [];

  add(resource: Resource) {
    this.resources.push(resource);
  }

  // 批量清理
  clear() {
    this.resources.forEach(r => r.dispose());
    this.resources = [];
  }

  // 单独清理
  remove(resource: Resource) {
    const index = this.resources.indexOf(resource);
    if (index > -1) {
      this.resources[index].dispose();
      this.resources.splice(index, 1);
    }
  }
}

// 4. 使用WeakRef（ES2021）
class Cache {
  private cache = new WeakMap<object, any>();

  set(key: object, value: any) {
    this.cache.set(key, new WeakRef(value));
  }

  get(key: object) {
    const ref = this.cache.get(key);
    return ref?.deref();
  }
}

// 5. 定期监控
setInterval(() => {
  if (performance.memory) {
    const { usedJSHeapSize } = performance.memory;
    const mb = (usedJSHeapSize / 1048576).toFixed(2);
    console.log(`Heap: ${mb} MB`);
  }
}, 30000);
```

---

### 19.4 长列表优化

**面试问题：如何优化长列表的渲染性能？**

**参考答案：**

**一、长列表优化原理**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      长列表优化原理                              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  传统渲染：显示全部项目                                           │
│  ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ... ┌─────┐           │
│  │Item1│ │Item2│ │Item3│ │Item4│ │Item5│     │ItemN│           │
│  └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘     └─────┘           │
│                                                                 │
│  虚拟滚动：只渲染可见项目                                         │
│  ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐                                       │
│  │Item1│ │Item2│ │Item3│   视口(visible)                        │
│  └─────┘ └─────┘ └─────┘                                       │
│                                                                 │
│  ┌─────┐ ┌─────┐                                                │
│  │Item │ │Item │   缓冲区域(buffer)                              │
│  └─────┘ └─────┘                                                │
│                                                                 │
│  原理：通过计算滚动位置，只渲染当前可见区域及其缓冲区的列表项      │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、手写虚拟列表**

```typescript
// 虚拟列表核心实现
class VirtualList<T> {
  private container: HTMLElement;
  private items: T[];
  private itemHeight: number;
  private visibleCount: number;
  private bufferCount: number;
  private scrollTop: number = 0;
  private renderStartIndex: number = 0;
  private renderEndIndex: number = 0;

  constructor(container: HTMLElement, options: VirtualListOptions<T>) {
    this.container = container;
    this.items = options.items;
    this.itemHeight = options.itemHeight;
    this.bufferCount = options.bufferCount || 3;

    this.init();
  }

  private init() {
    // 计算可见项数量
    this.visibleCount = Math.ceil(this.container.clientHeight / this.itemHeight);

    // 计算渲染范围
    this.updateRenderRange();

    // 绑定滚动事件
    this.container.addEventListener('scroll', this.handleScroll);
  }

  private handleScroll = () => {
    this.scrollTop = this.container.scrollTop;
    this.updateRenderRange();
    this.render();
  };

  private updateRenderRange() {
    // 计算可见区域的起始索引
    this.renderStartIndex = Math.max(
      0,
      Math.floor(this.scrollTop / this.itemHeight) - this.bufferCount
    );

    // 计算可见区域的结束索引
    this.renderEndIndex = Math.min(
      this.items.length,
      this.renderStartIndex + this.visibleCount + this.bufferCount * 2
    );
  }

  private render() {
    // 清空容器
    this.container.innerHTML = '';

    // 创建内部容器用于撑起高度
    const totalHeight = this.items.length * this.itemHeight;
    const spacer = document.createElement('div');
    spacer.style.height = `${totalHeight}px`;
    spacer.style.position = 'relative';
    this.container.appendChild(spacer);

    // 渲染可见项
    for (let i = this.renderStartIndex; i < this.renderEndIndex; i++) {
      const item = this.items[i];
      const itemElement = this.createItemElement(item, i);
      itemElement.style.position = 'absolute';
      itemElement.style.top = `${i * this.itemHeight}px`;
      itemElement.style.left = '0';
      itemElement.style.width = '100%';
      itemElement.style.height = `${this.itemHeight}px`;
      this.container.appendChild(itemElement);
    }
  }

  protected createItemElement(item: T, index: number): HTMLElement {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.textContent = `Item ${index}: ${JSON.stringify(item)}`;
    return div;
  }

  // 更新数据
  setItems(items: T[]) {
    this.items = items;
    this.updateRenderRange();
    this.render();
  }

  // 销毁
  destroy() {
    this.container.removeEventListener('scroll', this.handleScroll);
    this.container.innerHTML = '';
  }
}

interface VirtualListOptions<T> {
  items: T[];
  itemHeight: number;
  bufferCount?: number;
}
```

**三、React虚拟列表**

```typescript
// 使用react-window
import { FixedSizeList, VariableSizeList } from 'react-window';
import AutoSizer from 'react-virtualized-auto-sizer';

// 固定高度列表
function FixedHeightList({ items }) {
  const Row = ({ index, style }) => (
    <div style={style} className="list-item">
      {items[index].name}
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div style={{ height: '500px' }}>
      <AutoSizer>
        {({ height, width }) => (
          <FixedSizeList
            height={height}
            width={width}
            itemCount={items.length}
            itemSize={50}
          >
            {Row}
          </FixedSizeList>
        )}
      </AutoSizer>
    </div>
  );
}

// 可变高度列表
function VariableHeightList({ items }) {
  const getItemSize = (index: number) => {
    // 根据内容计算高度
    const baseHeight = 50;
    const extraLines = Math.floor(items[index].description.length / 50);
    return baseHeight + extraLines * 20;
  };

  const Row = ({ index, style }) => (
    <div style={style} className="list-item">
      <h3>{items[index].title}</h3>
      <p>{items[index].description}</p>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div style={{ height: '500px' }}>
      <AutoSizer>
        {({ height, width }) => (
          <VariableSizeList
            height={height}
            width={width}
            itemCount={items.length}
            itemSize={getItemSize}
          >
            {Row}
          </VariableSizeList>
        )}
      </AutoSizer>
    </div>
  );
}

// 无限滚动列表
function InfiniteList({ fetchMore, items, hasMore }) {
  const [listHeight, setListHeight] = useState(500);
  const [listWidth, setListWidth] = useState('100%');

  const loadMoreItems = ({ stopIndex }) => {
    if (hasMore && stopIndex >= items.length - 5) {
      fetchMore();
    }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ height: listHeight }}>
      <AutoSizer>
        {({ height, width }) => (
          <FixedSizeList
            height={height}
            width={width}
            itemCount={hasMore ? items.length + 1 : items.length}
            itemSize={50}
            onItemsRendered={loadMoreItems}
          >
            {({ index, style }) => {
              if (index >= items.length) {
                return <div style={style}>Loading...</div>;
              }
              return <div style={style}>{items[index].name}</div>;
            }}
          </FixedSizeList>
        )}
      </AutoSizer>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```typescript
<template>

    :item-size="50"
    key-field="id"
    v-slot="{ item }"

    <div class="item">
      {{ item.name }}

</template>

export default {

    RecycleScroller,
    DynamicScroller

      items: []
    };

.scroller {
  height: 500px;
}
</style>
```

**五、长列表优化技巧**

```typescript
// 1. 数据懒加载
async function loadData(page: number) {
  const response = await fetch(`/api/items?page=${page}&size=50`);
  const newItems = await response.json();

  setItems(prev => [...prev, ...newItems]);
}

// 2. 列表项优化
const ListItem = React.memo(({ item }) => {
  return (
    <div className="list-item">
      <img
        src={item.thumbnail}
        loading="lazy" // 懒加载图片
        alt={item.title}
      />
      <div>{item.title}</div>
    </div>
  );
}, (prevProps, nextProps) => {
  // 自定义比较
  return prevProps.item.id === nextProps.item.id;
});

// 3. 下拉刷新 + 上拉加载
function VirtualListWithRefresh() {
  const [items, setItems] = useState([]);
  const [refreshing, setRefreshing] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const onRefresh = async () => {
    setRefreshing(true);
    const data = await fetchNewData();
    setItems(data);
    setRefreshing(false);
  };

  const onLoadMore = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    const moreData = await fetchMoreData(items.length);
    setItems(prev => [...prev, ...moreData]);
    setLoading(false);
  };

  return (
    <PullToRefresh
      refreshing={refreshing}
      onRefresh={onRefresh}
    >
      <VirtualList
        items={items}
        onEndReached={onLoadMore}
        loading={loading}
      />
    </PullToRefresh>
  );
}

// 4. 搜索过滤优化
function useFilteredList(items, filter) {
  const [filteredItems, setFilteredItems] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    // 防抖过滤
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      const filtered = items.filter(item =>
        item.name.toLowerCase().includes(filter.toLowerCase())
      );
      setFilteredItems(filtered);
    }, 300);

    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [items, filter]);

  return filteredItems;
}

// 5. 分组列表
function GroupedList({ items }) {
  const groups = useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map();
    items.forEach(item => {
      const key = item.category;
      if (!map.has(key)) {
        map.set(key, []);
      }
      map.get(key).push(item);
    });
    return Array.from(map.entries());
  }, [items]);

  return (
    <SectionList
      sections={groups.map(([title, data]) => ({ title, data }))}
      renderItem={({ item }) => <ListItem item={item} />}
      renderSectionHeader={({ section }) => (
        <div className="section-header">{section.title}</div>
      )}
    />
  );
}
```

### 19.5 图片加载优化

**面试问题：有哪些图片加载优化策略？**

**参考答案：**

**一、图片优化策略总览**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      图片优化策略                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  1. 格式优化                                                    │
│     JPEG -> WebP -> AVIF                                       │
│     PNG -> WebP                                                 │
│                                                                 │
│  2. 尺寸优化                                                    │
│     响应式图片 - srcset                                         │
│     缩略图 - 适当尺寸                                            │
│                                                                 │
│  3. 加载优化                                                    │
│     懒加载 - loading="lazy"                                    │
│     预加载 - preload                                            │
│     渐进式加载                                                   │
│                                                                 │
│  4. 缓存优化                                                    │
│     强缓存                                                      │
│     CDN                                                        │
│                                                                 │
│  5. 显示优化                                                    │
│     骨架屏                                                      │
│     占位图                                                      │
│     模糊加载                                                   │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、响应式图片**

```typescript
// 1. srcset属性
<img
  src="image-800.jpg"
  srcset="
    image-400.jpg 400w,
    image-800.jpg 800w,
    image-1200.jpg 1200w,
    image-1600.jpg 1600w
  "
  sizes="
    (max-width: 600px) 400px,
    (max-width: 1200px) 800px,
    1200px
  "
  alt="Responsive image"
/>

// 2. picture元素
<picture>
  <source
    type="image/avif"
    srcset="image.avif"
  />
  <source
    type="image/webp"
    srcset="image.webp"
  />
  <img
    src="image.jpg"
    alt="Image"
  />
</picture>

// 3. React组件封装
function ResponsiveImage({
  src,
  alt,
  sizes = '100vw',
  placeholder,
  lazy = true
}) {
  const [loaded, setLoaded] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);

  const srcSet = generateSrcSet(src);
  const baseSrc = getBaseSrc(src);

  return (
    <div className="image-container">
      {!loaded && !error && (
        <div className="placeholder">
          {placeholder || <Skeleton />}
        </div>
      )}
      <img
        src={baseSrc}
        srcSet={srcSet}
        sizes={sizes}
        alt={alt}
        loading={lazy ? 'lazy' : 'eager'}
        onLoad={() => setLoaded(true)}
        onError={() => setError(true)}
        className={`image ${loaded ? 'loaded' : ''}`}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

**三、图片懒加载**

```typescript
// 1. 原生懒加载
<img loading="lazy" src="image.jpg" alt="Lazy loaded" />

// 2. Intersection Observer实现
function useLazyLoad(options = {}) {
  const [isLoaded, setIsLoaded] = useState(false);
  const [isInView, setIsInView] = useState(false);
  const imgRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
      (entries) => {
        entries.forEach((entry) => {
          if (entry.isIntersecting) {
            setIsInView(true);
            observer.disconnect();
          }
        });
      },
      {
        rootMargin: options.rootMargin || '100px',
        threshold: options.threshold || 0
      }
    );

    if (imgRef.current) {
      observer.observe(imgRef.current);
    }

    return () => observer.disconnect();
  }, []);

  return { imgRef, isInView, isLoaded, setIsLoaded };
}

// 使用
function LazyImage({ src, alt, ...props }) {
  const { imgRef, isInView, isLoaded, setIsLoaded } = useLazyLoad();

  return (
    <img
      ref={imgRef}
      src={isInView ? src : undefined}
      alt={alt}
      onLoad={() => setIsLoaded(true)}
      className={isLoaded ? 'loaded' : 'loading'}
      {...props}
    />
  );
}

// 3. 滚动位置计算
function scrollLazyLoad() {
  const images = document.querySelectorAll('[data-src]');

  const loadImage = (image) => {
    const src = image.getAttribute('data-src');
    if (!src) return;

    image.src = src;
    image.removeAttribute('data-src');
  };

  const handleScroll = throttle(() => {
    images.forEach(image => {
      const rect = image.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (rect.top < window.innerHeight + 100) {
        loadImage(image);
      }
    });
  }, 200);

  window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll);
}
```

```typescript
function BlurPlaceholder({ src, blurSrc, alt }) {

  return (
    <div className="image-wrapper">
      <img
        src={blurSrc}
        alt={alt}

// CSS
```

**五、图片压缩与格式转换**

```typescript
// 1. 图片CDN
function getOptimizedImageUrl(
  originalUrl: string,
  options: ImageOptions
): string {
  const cdnBase = 'https://cdn.example.com';
  const {
    width,
    height,
    format = 'webp',
    quality = 80
  } = options;

  const params = new URLSearchParams();
  if (width) params.set('w', width.toString());
  if (height) params.set('h', height.toString());
  if (format) params.set('fm', format);
  if (quality) params.set('q', quality.toString());

  return `${cdnBase}/image/${originalUrl}?${params.toString()}`;
}

// 2. 浏览器端图片压缩
async function compressImage(
  file: File,
  options: CompressionOptions = {}
): Promise<Blob> {
  const {
    maxWidth = 1920,
    maxHeight = 1080,
    quality = 0.8,
    format = 'image/webp'
  } = options;

  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const img = new Image();
    img.onload = () => {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      let { width, height } = img;

      // 计算缩放比例
      if (width > maxWidth) {
        height = (height * maxWidth) / width;
        width = maxWidth;
      }
      if (height > maxHeight) {
        width = (width * maxHeight) / height;
        height = maxHeight;
      }

      canvas.width = width;
      canvas.height = height;

      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      ctx?.drawImage(img, 0, 0, width, height);

      canvas.toBlob(
        (blob) => {
          if (blob) resolve(blob);
          else reject(new Error('Compression failed'));
        },
        format,
        quality
      );
    };

    img.onerror = reject;
    img.src = URL.createObjectURL(file);
  });
}

// 3. WebP/AVIF检测与使用
function getSupportedFormat(): string {
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  canvas.width = 1;
  canvas.height = 1;

  if (canvas.toDataURL('image/avif').startsWith('data:image/avif')) {
    return 'avif';
  }
  if (canvas.toDataURL('image/webp').startsWith('data:image/webp')) {
    return 'webp';
  }
  return 'jpeg';
}
```

### 19.6 接口性能优化

**面试问题：如何优化前端接口调用性能？**

**参考答案：**

**一、接口性能优化策略**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      接口性能优化                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  1. 请求优化                                                    │
│     - 减少请求数量（合并请求）                                   │
│     - 减少请求数据（按需获取）                                   │
│     - 请求优先级                                                 │
│     - 请求缓存                                                   │
│                                                                 │
│  2. 网络优化                                                    │
│     - CDN加速                                                   │
│     - HTTP/2 multiplexing                                      │
│     - Gzip压缩                                                  │
│     - 减少DNS查询                                               │
│                                                                 │
│  3. 并发优化                                                    │
│     - 并发请求                                                  │
│     - 请求依赖管理                                              │
│     - 熔断降级                                                  │
│                                                                 │
│  4. 响应优化                                                    │
│     - 分页加载                                                  │
│     - 增量更新                                                  │
│     - 数据压缩                                                  │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、请求合并与批量处理**

```typescript
// 1. 请求合并 - 相同请求
class RequestBatcher {
  private pending = new Map<string, Promise<any>>();
  private timers = new Map<string, NodeJS.Timeout>();

  async request(key: string, fetcher: () => Promise<any>): Promise<any> {
    // 如果已有相同请求在进行，直接等待
    if (this.pending.has(key)) {
      return this.pending.get(key);
    }

    // 创建新请求
    const promise = fetcher();
    this.pending.set(key, promise);

    try {
      return await promise;
    } finally {
      this.pending.delete(key);
    }
  }

  // 批量请求
  async batch<T>(
    requests: { key: string; fetcher: () => Promise<T> }[]
  ): Promise<Map<string, T>> {
    const results = new Map<string, T>();

    await Promise.all(
      requests.map(async ({ key, fetcher }) => {
        const result = await this.request(key, fetcher);
        results.set(key, result);
      })
    );

    return results;
  }
}

// 2. 多次请求合并为一次
async function getUserData(userIds: string[]) {
  const batcher = new RequestBatcher();

  // 使用批量接口
  const users = await batcher.batch(
    userIds.map(id => ({
      key: `user:${id}`,
      fetcher: () => fetch(`/api/users/batch?ids=${userIds.join(',')}`)
    }))
  );

  return users;
}
```

**三、请求缓存**

```typescript
// 1. 内存缓存
class MemoryCache {
  private cache = new Map<string, { data: any; expiry: number }>();

  get<T>(key: string): T | null {
    const item = this.cache.get(key);
    if (!item) return null;

    if (Date.now() > item.expiry) {
      this.cache.delete(key);
      return null;
    }

    return item.data as T;
  }

  set<T>(key: string, data: T, ttl: number = 60000) {
    this.cache.set(key, {
      data,
      expiry: Date.now() + ttl
    });
  }

  delete(key: string) {
    this.cache.delete(key);
  }

  clear() {
    this.cache.clear();
  }
}

// 2. 缓存装饰器
function cached(ttl: number = 60000) {
  const cache = new MemoryCache();

  return function (
    target: any,
    propertyKey: string,
    descriptor: PropertyDescriptor
  ) {
    const original = descriptor.value;

    descriptor.value = async function (...args: any[]) {
      const key = `${propertyKey}:${JSON.stringify(args)}`;
      const cachedData = cache.get(key);

      if (cachedData) {
        return cachedData;
      }

      const result = await original.apply(this, args);
      cache.set(key, result, ttl);
      return result;
    };

    return descriptor;
  };
}

// 使用
class UserService {
  @cached(60000) // 缓存1分钟
  async getUser(id: string) {
    return fetch(`/api/users/${id}`);
  }
}
```

**四、请求去重与防抖**

```typescript
// 1. 请求去重
class RequestDeduplicator {
  private inFlight = new Map<string, Promise<any>>();

  async request<T>(
    key: string,
    fetcher: () => Promise<T>
  ): Promise<T> {
    // 如果有正在进行的相同请求
    if (this.inFlight.has(key)) {
      return this.inFlight.get(key);
    }

    // 创建新请求
    const promise = fetcher().finally(() => {
      this.inFlight.delete(key);
    });

    this.inFlight.set(key, promise);
    return promise;
  }
}

// 2. 防抖请求
function useDebouncedSearch(searchFn: (query: string) => Promise<any>) {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const debouncedSearch = useMemo(
    () => debounce(async (query: string) => {
      if (!query.trim()) return;
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const result = await searchFn(query);
        return result;
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }, 300),
    [searchFn]
  );

  return { loading, search: debouncedSearch };
}

// 3. 节流请求
function useThrottledRefresh(refreshFn: () => Promise<void>) {
  const [refreshing, setRefreshing] = useState(false);

  const throttledRefresh = useMemo(
    () => throttle(async () => {
      if (refreshing) return;
      setRefreshing(true);
      try {
        await refreshFn();
      } finally {
        setRefreshing(false);
      }
    }, 1000),
    [refreshFn]
  );

  return { refreshing, refresh: throttledRefresh };
}
```

**五、并发与依赖管理**

```typescript
// 1. 并发请求优化
async function loadPageData() {
  // 串行 - 慢
  const user = await fetch('/api/user').then(r => r.json());
  const orders = await fetch('/api/orders').then(r => r.json());
  const products = await fetch('/api/products').then(r => r.json());

  // 并行 - 快
  const [user, orders, products] = await Promise.all([
    fetch('/api/user').then(r => r.json()),
    fetch('/api/orders').then(r => r.json()),
    fetch('/api/products').then(r => r.json())
  ]);

  return { user, orders, products };
}

// 2. 请求依赖管理
async function loadDataWithDependencies() {
  // 第一层：用户信息（无依赖）
  const userPromise = fetch('/api/user').then(r => r.json());

  const user = await userPromise;

  // 第二层：依赖用户ID的请求
  const [orders, cart] = await Promise.all([
    fetch(`/api/users/${user.id}/orders`).then(r => r.json()),
    fetch(`/api/users/${user.id}/cart`).then(r => r.json())
  ]);

  return { user, orders, cart };
}

// 3. 关键请求优先
async function loadCriticalData() {
  const critical = fetch('/api/critical').then(r => r.json());
  const nonCritical = fetch('/api/non-critical').then(r => r.json());

  // 等待关键数据
  const criticalData = await critical;

  // 非关键数据在后台加载
  nonCritical.then(data => updateUI(data));

  return criticalData;
}
```

**六、错误处理与重试**

```typescript
// 1. 自动重试
async function fetchWithRetry<T>(
  url: string,
  options: RequestInit = {},
  maxRetries: number = 3
): Promise<T> {
  let lastError: Error;

  for (let attempt = 0; attempt < maxRetries; attempt++) {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(url, options);

      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
      }

      return await response.json();
    } catch (error) {
      lastError = error as Error;

      // 指数退避
      if (attempt < maxRetries - 1) {
        const delay = Math.pow(2, attempt) * 1000;
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
      }
    }
  }

  throw lastError!;
}

// 2. 熔断器模式
class CircuitBreaker {
  private failures = 0;
  private lastFailureTime = 0;
  private state: 'closed' | 'open' | 'half-open' = 'closed';

  constructor(
    private threshold: number = 5,
    private timeout: number = 60000
  ) {}

  async execute<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>): Promise<T> {
    if (this.state === 'open') {
      if (Date.now() - this.lastFailureTime > this.timeout) {
        this.state = 'half-open';
      } else {
        throw new Error('Circuit breaker is open');
      }
    }

    try {
      const result = await fn();
      this.onSuccess();
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.onFailure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  private onSuccess() {
    this.failures = 0;
    this.state = 'closed';
  }

  private onFailure() {
    this.failures++;
    this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();

    if (this.failures >= this.threshold) {
      this.state = 'open';
    }
  }
}
```

---

### 19.7 缓存策略设计

**面试问题：如何设计前端缓存策略？**

**参考答案：**

**一、缓存层次架构**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      前端缓存层次                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │  浏览器缓存                                               │  │
│  │  ├─ HTTP缓存                                              │  │
│  │  │   ├─ 强缓存 (Cache-Control, Expires)                  │  │
│  │  │   └─ 协商缓存 (ETag, Last-Modified)                   │  │
│  │  │                                                       │  │
│  │  ├─ Service Worker缓存                                    │  │
│  │  │   ├─ Cache API                                        │  │
│  │  │   └─ 离线支持                                          │  │
│  │  │                                                       │  │
│  │  └─ 存储API                                              │  │
│  │      ├─ localStorage                                      │  │
│  │      ├─ sessionStorage                                    │  │
│  │      ├─ IndexedDB                                         │  │
│  │      └─ Cache API                                         │  │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                 │
│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
│  │  内存缓存                                                 │  │
│  │  ├─ 变量缓存                                              │  │
│  │  ├─ React/Vue状态                                         │  │
│  │  └─ 组件缓存                                              │  │
│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
│                                                                 │
│  缓存优先级： 内存 > Service Worker > HTTP > 网络请求            │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、HTTP缓存策略**

```typescript
// 1. 强缓存配置
// 静态资源 - 长期缓存
Cache-Control: public, max-age=31536000, immutable

// HTML - 协商缓存
Cache-Control: no-cache

// 图片 - 长期缓存
Cache-Control: public, max-age=86400

// 2. 缓存策略配置示例
const cacheStrategies = {
  // 静态资源：长期缓存
  static: {
    '**/*.js': {
      cacheControl: 'public, max-age=31536000, immutable'
    },
    '**/*.css': {
      cacheControl: 'public, max-age=31536000, immutable'
    },
    '**/*.woff2': {
      cacheControl: 'public, max-age=31536000, immutable'
    }
  },

  // 图片：长期缓存 + 重新验证
  image: {
    '**/*.{jpg,png,gif}': {
      cacheControl: 'public, max-age=86400',
      vary: 'Accept'
    }
  },

  // API：按类型缓存
  api: {
    '/api/user/profile': {
      cacheControl: 'private, max-age=3600'
    },
    '/api/config': {
      cacheControl: 'public, max-age=300'
    },
    '/api/list': {
      cacheControl: 'no-cache'
    }
  }
};
```

**三、Service Worker缓存**

```typescript
// Service Worker实现
const CACHE_NAME = 'app-v1';
const STATIC_ASSETS = [
  '/',
  '/index.html',
  '/static/js/main.js',
  '/static/css/main.css',
  '/manifest.json'
];

// 安装阶段 - 缓存静态资源
self.addEventListener('install', (event) => {
  event.waitUntil(
    caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then((cache) => {
      return cache.addAll(STATIC_ASSETS);
    })
  );
});

// 激活阶段 - 清理旧缓存
self.addEventListener('activate', (event) => {
  event.waitUntil(
    caches.keys().then((cacheNames) => {
      return Promise.all(
        cacheNames
          .filter((name) => name !== CACHE_NAME)
          .map((name) => caches.delete(name))
      );
    })
  );
});

// 请求拦截 - 缓存策略
self.addEventListener('fetch', (event) => {
  const { request } = event;
  const url = new URL(request.url);

  // 网络优先策略 - API请求
  if (url.pathname.startsWith('/api/')) {
    event.respondWith(networkFirst(request));
    return;
  }

  // 缓存优先策略 - 静态资源
  if (isStaticAsset(url.pathname)) {
    event.respondWith(cacheFirst(request));
    return;
  }

  // 后备策略 - 其他请求
  event.respondWith(networkWithFallback(request));
});

// 缓存优先策略
async function cacheFirst(request) {
  const cached = await caches.match(request);
  if (cached) {
    return cached;
  }

  try {
    const response = await fetch(request);
    if (response.ok) {
      const cache = await caches.open(CACHE_NAME);
      cache.put(request, response.clone());
    }
    return response;
  } catch (error) {
    return caches.match('/offline.html');
  }
}

// 网络优先策略
async function networkFirst(request) {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(request);
    if (response.ok) {
      const cache = await caches.open(CACHE_NAME);
      cache.put(request, response.clone());
    }
    return response;
  } catch (error) {
    const cached = await caches.match(request);
    return cached || new Response('Offline', { status: 503 });
  }
}

// 仅缓存策略
async function cacheOnly(request) {
  const cached = await caches.match(request);
  return cached || new Response('Not Found', { status: 404 });
}

// 仅网络策略
async function networkOnly(request) {
  return fetch(request);
}
```

**四、应用层缓存**

```typescript
// 1. React Query / SWR
import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider, useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';

const queryClient = new QueryClient({
  defaultOptions: {
    queries: {
      // 缓存时间
      staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000,
      // 缓存保留时间
      cacheTime: 10 * 60 * 1000,
      // 重试
      retry: 3,
      // 后台刷新
      refetchOnWindowFocus: false
    }
  }
});

function UserProfile({ userId }) {
  const { data, isLoading, error } = useQuery({
    queryKey: ['user', userId],
    queryFn: () => fetch(`/api/users/${userId}`).then(r => r.json()),
    // 缓存5分钟
    staleTime: 5 * 60 * 1000,
    // 重新获取
    refetchOnMount: false
  });

  if (isLoading) return <Loading />;
  if (error) return <Error />;

  return <div>{data.name}</div>;
}

// 2. Zustand持久化缓存
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';

interface UserState {
  user: User | null;
  setUser: (user: User | null) => void;
}

const useUserStore = create<UserState>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      user: null,
      setUser: (user) => set({ user })
    }),
    {
      name: 'user-storage',
      partialize: (state) => ({ user: state.user })
    }
  )
);

// 3. 自定义缓存Hook
function useCachedData<T>(
  key: string,
  fetcher: () => Promise<T>,
  options: CacheOptions = {}
) {
  const { ttl = 60000, storage = 'memory' } = options;
  const [data, setData] = useState<T | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<Error | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const cache = getCache(storage);
    const cached = cache.get<T>(key);

    if (cached) {
      setData(cached);
      setLoading(false);
      return;
    }

    fetcher()
      .then((result) => {
        cache.set(key, result, ttl);
        setData(result);
      })
      .catch(setError)
      .finally(() => setLoading(false));
  }, [key, fetcher, ttl, storage]);

  const refresh = useCallback(async () => {
    const result = await fetcher();
    const cache = getCache(storage);
    cache.set(key, result, ttl);
    setData(result);
  }, [key, fetcher, ttl, storage]);

  return { data, loading, error, refresh };
}
```

**五、缓存更新策略**

```typescript
// 1. 缓存失效策略
class CacheManager {
  private cache: Map<string, CacheEntry>;

  set(key: string, value: any, ttl?: number) {
    this.cache.set(key, {
      value,
      expiry: ttl ? Date.now() + ttl : null
    });
  }

  invalidate(pattern: string) {
    const regex = new RegExp(pattern);
    for (const key of this.cache.keys()) {
      if (regex.test(key)) {
        this.cache.delete(key);
      }
    }
  }

  invalidatePrefix(prefix: string) {
    for (const key of this.cache.keys()) {
      if (key.startsWith(prefix)) {
        this.cache.delete(key);
      }
    }
  }
}

// 2. 乐观更新
function useOptimisticUpdate() {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  const updateData = useMutation(
    (newData) => updateAPI(newData),
    {
      onMutate: async (newData) => {
        // 取消正在进行的查询
        await queryClient.cancelQueries(['data']);

        // 保存之前的值
        const previousData = queryClient.getQueryData(['data']);

        // 乐观更新
        queryClient.setQueryData(['data'], (old) => ({
          ...old,
          ...newData
        }));

        return { previousData };
      },
      onError: (err, newData, context) => {
        // 回滚
        queryClient.setQueryData(['data'], context?.previousData);
      },
      onSettled: () => {
        // 重新获取
        queryClient.invalidateQueries(['data']);
      }
    }
  );

  return updateData;
}
```

### 20.1 构建工具选型与配置

**面试问题：如何选择和配置前端构建工具？**

**参考答案：**

**一、构建工具对比**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      构建工具对比                               │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  Webpack                    Vite                   Rollup      │
│  ─────────                  ─────                  ──────      │
│  生态成熟  ★★★★★           开发体验 ★★★★★          打包质量 ★★★★★ │
│  配置复杂  ★★★☆☆           配置简单 ★★★★★          功能专注 ★★★★☆ │
│  构建速度  ★★☆☆☆           构建速度 ★★★★★          生态较弱  ★★★☆☆ │
│  插件丰富  ★★★★★           插件生态 ★★★★☆          学习曲线 ★★★☆☆ │
│                                                                 │
│  适用场景：                   适用场景：               适用场景： │
│  - 大型复杂项目               - 新项目                 - 库打包    │
│  - 需要精细控制               - 追求开发体验           - 小型项目  │
│  - 老项目维护                 - 快速原型                - 简单打包  │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、Webpack深入配置**

```javascript
// webpack.config.js - 完整配置示例
const path = require('path');
const HtmlWebpackPlugin = require('html-webpack-plugin');
const MiniCssExtractPlugin = require('mini-css-extract-plugin');
const CssMinimizerPlugin = require('css-minimizer-webpack-plugin');
const TerserPlugin = require('terser-webpack-plugin');
const { ModuleFederationPlugin } = require('webpack').container;
const CompressionPlugin = require('compression-webpack-plugin');
const { CleanWebpackPlugin } = require('clean-webpack-plugin');

module.exports = (env, argv) => {
  const isProduction = argv.mode === 'production';

  return {
    // 入口配置
    entry: {
      main: './src/index.tsx',
      vendor: './src/vendor.tsx',
      // 多页面
      admin: './src/pages/admin/index.tsx'
    },

    // 输出配置
    output: {
      path: path.resolve(__dirname, 'dist'),
      filename: isProduction
        ? '[name].[contenthash].js'
        : '[name].js',
      chunkFilename: isProduction
        ? '[name].[contenthash].chunk.js'
        : '[name].chunk.js',
      assetModuleFilename: 'assets/[hash][ext][query]',
      clean: true,
      publicPath: '/'
    },

    // 解析配置
    resolve: {
      extensions: ['.tsx', '.ts', '.jsx', '.js', '.json'],
      alias: {
        '@': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src'),
        '@components': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src/components'),
        '@utils': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src/utils'),
        '@hooks': path.resolve(__dirname, 'src/hooks'),
        // 第三方库别名
        'react': path.resolve(__dirname, 'node_modules/react'),
        'lodash': path.resolve(__dirname, 'node_modules/lodash-es')
      },
      // 解析模块时搜索的目录
      modules: [
        path.resolve(__dirname, 'src'),
        'node_modules'
      ]
    },

    // 模块配置
    module: {
      rules: [
        // TypeScript
        {
          test: /\.tsx?$/,
          exclude: /node_modules/,
          use: [
            {
              loader: 'babel-loader',
              options: {
                cacheDirectory: true,
                presets: [
                  '@babel/preset-typescript',
                  ['@babel/preset-react', { runtime: 'automatic' }],
                  ['@babel/preset-env', { modules: false }]
                ]
              }
            },
            // ts-loader作为类型检查
            {
              loader: 'ts-loader',
              options: {
                transpileOnly: true,
                happyPackMode: true
              }
            }
          ]
        },

        // CSS
        {
          test: /\.css$/,
          use: [
            isProduction ? MiniCssExtractPlugin.loader : 'style-loader',
            {
              loader: 'css-loader',
              options: {
                modules: {
                  auto: (resourcePath) => resourcePath.endsWith('.module.css'),
                  localIdentName: isProduction
                    ? '[hash:base64]'
                    : '[name]__[local]--[hash:base64:5]'
                }
              }
            },
            {
              loader: 'postcss-loader',
              options: {
                postcssOptions: {
                  plugins: [
                    'postcss-preset-env',
                    'autoprefixer'
                  ]
                }
              }
            }
          ]
        },

        // 图片
        {
          test: /\.(png|jpe?g|gif|svg|webp)$/i,
          type: 'asset',
          parser: {
            dataUrlCondition: {
              maxSize: 8 * 1024 // 8KB以下转base64
            }
          }
        },

        // 字体
        {
          test: /\.(woff|woff2|eot|ttf|otf)$/i,
          type: 'asset/resource'
        },

        // 文件
        {
          test: /\.(mp4|webm|ogg|mp3|wav|flac|aac)$/i,
          type: 'asset/resource'
        },

        // CSV/JSON
        {
          test: /\.(csv|json)$/i,
          type: 'asset/resource'
        }
      ]
    },

    // 插件配置
    plugins: [
      new CleanWebpackPlugin(),

      new HtmlWebpackPlugin({
        template: './public/index.html',
        filename: 'index.html',
        chunks: ['main', 'vendor'],
        minify: isProduction ? {
          removeComments: true,
          collapseWhitespace: true,
          removeAttributeQuotes: true
        } : false
      }),

      new MiniCssExtractPlugin({
        filename: isProduction
          ? '[name].[contenthash].css'
          : '[name].css'
      }),

      new CompressionPlugin({
        algorithm: 'gzip',
        test: /\.(js|css|html|svg)$/,
        threshold: 10240,
        minRatio: 0.8
      }),

      // 模块联邦
      new ModuleFederationPlugin({
        name: 'host',
        remotes: {
          app1: 'app1@http://localhost:3001/remoteEntry.js',
          app2: 'app2@http://localhost:3002/remoteEntry.js'
        },
        shared: {
          react: { singleton: true, requiredVersion: '^18.0.0' },
          'react-dom': { singleton: true, requiredVersion: '^18.0.0' }
        }
      })
    ],

    // 优化配置
    optimization: {
      minimize: isProduction,
      minimizer: [
        new TerserPlugin({
          terserOptions: {
            compress: {
              drop_console: isProduction,
              drop_debugger: isProduction
            }
          }
        }),
        new CssMinimizerPlugin()
      ],

      // 代码分割
      splitChunks: {
        chunks: 'all',
        maxInitialRequests: 25,
        maxAsyncRequests: 25,
        minSize: 20000,
        cacheGroups: {
          // node_modules
          vendor: {
            test: /[\\/]node_modules[\\/]/,
            name: 'vendors',
            chunks: 'all',
            priority: 10
          },
          // React生态
          react: {
            test: /[\\/]node_modules[\\/](react|react-dom|react-router)[\\/]/,
            name: 'react',
            chunks: 'all',
            priority: 20
          },
          // 公共模块
          common: {
            name: 'common',
            minChunks: 2,
            priority: 5
          }
        }
      },

      // 运行时提取
      runtimeChunk: 'single',

      // 模块标识符
      moduleIds: 'deterministic'
    },

    // 开发服务器
    devServer: {
      static: {
        directory: path.join(__dirname, 'public')
      },
      port: 3000,
      hot: true,
      historyApiFallback: true,
      proxy: {
        '/api': {
          target: 'http://localhost:8080',
          changeOrigin: true,
          secure: false
        }
      },
      // 性能提示
      client: {
        overlay: {
          errors: true,
          warnings: false
        }
      }
    },

    // 性能配置
    performance: {
      hints: isProduction ? 'warning' : false,
      maxEntrypointSize: 512000,
      maxAssetSize: 512000
    },

    // 调试
    devtool: isProduction ? 'source-map' : 'eval-cheap-module-source-map',

    // 统计信息
    stats: {
      colors: true,
      modules: false,
      children: false
    }
  };
};
```

**三、Vite深入配置**

```typescript
// vite.config.ts
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import path from 'path';
import { resolve } from 'path';

// 类型定义
/// <reference types="vite/client" />

export default defineConfig({
  // 基础路径
  base: '/',

  // 解析
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),
      '@components': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/components'),
      '@utils': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/utils')
    },
    extensions: ['.mjs', '.js', '.ts', '.jsx', '.tsx', '.json']
  },

  // 插件
  plugins: [
    react({
      // Fast Refresh
      fastRefresh: true,
      // JSX
      jsxImportSource: 'react',
      // Babel配置
      babel: {
        parserOpts: {
          plugins: ['decorators-legacy']
        }
      }
    })
  ],

  // CSS
  css: {
    modules: {
      localsConvention: 'camelCase'
    },
    postcss: './postcss.config.js',
    preprocessorOptions: {
      scss: {
        additionalData: `@import "@/styles/variables.scss";`
      },
      less: {
        javascriptEnabled: true
      }
    }
  },

  // JSON
  json: {
    namedExports: true
  },

  // 依赖优化
  optimizeDeps: {
    include: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
    exclude: ['lodash-es']
  },

  // 构建
  build: {
    target: 'es2015',
    outDir: 'dist',
    assetsDir: 'assets',
    sourcemap: false,
    minify: 'terser',
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 500,
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          'react-vendor': ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router'],
          'utils': ['lodash-es', 'axios', 'dayjs'],
          'ui': ['antd', '@ant-design/icons']
        },
        // 入口
        entryFileNames: 'js/[name].[hash].js',
        chunkFileNames: 'js/[name].[hash].js',
        assetFileNames: 'assets/[name].[hash][extname]',
        // 分隔符
        chunkFileNames: (chunkInfo) => {
          return 'js/[name].[hash].js';
        }
      },
      // 外部
      external: ['lodash'],
      // 插件
      plugins: []
    },
    // 压缩
    terserOptions: {
      compress: {
        drop_console: true,
        drop_debugger: true
      }
    },
    // 报表
    reportCompressedSize: true,
    // 禁用CSS代码分割
    cssCodeSplit: true
  },

  // 服务器
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    open: true,
    https: false,
    proxy: {
      '/api': {
        target: 'http://localhost:8080',
        changeOrigin: true,
        rewrite: (path) => path.replace(/^\/api/, '')
      }
    },
    hmr: {
      overlay: true
    }
  },

  // 预览
  preview: {
    port: 4173,
    proxy: {
      '/api': 'http://localhost:8080'
    }
  },

  // 环境变量
  envPrefix: 'VITE_',
  envFiles: [
    '.env',
    '.env.local',
    `.env.${process.env.NODE_ENV}`
  ]
});
```

### 20.2 代码质量保证

**面试问题：如何保证前端代码质量？**

**参考答案：**

**一、代码质量保障体系**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      代码质量保障体系                           │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  ┌─────────┐  ┌─────────┐  ┌─────────┐  ┌─────────┐          │
│  │ 代码规范 │  │ 代码检查│  │ 代码测试│  │ 代码审查│          │
│  │ (ESLint)│  │ (Prettier)│  │ (Jest) │  │ (Review)│          │
│  └─────────┘  └─────────┘  └─────────┘  └─────────┘          │
│       │            │            │            │                 │
│       └────────────┴────────────┴────────────┘                 │
│                           │                                     │
│                           ▼                                     │
│              ┌─────────────────────┐                            │
│              │     CI/CD流程       │                            │
│              └─────────────────────┘                            │
│                           │                                     │
│                           ▼                                     │
│              ┌─────────────────────┐                            │
│              │    质量监控        │                            │
│              └─────────────────────┘                            │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、ESLint配置**

```javascript
// .eslintrc.js
module.exports = {
  // 根目录
  root: true,

  // 解析器
  parser: '@typescript-eslint/parser',
  parserOptions: {
    ecmaVersion: 2021,
    sourceType: 'module',

      jsx: true
    }
  },

  // 插件
  plugins: [
    '@typescript-eslint',
    'react',
    'react-hooks',
    'jsx-a11y',
    'import',
    'prettier'
  ],

  // 继承配置
  extends: [
    'eslint:recommended',
    'plugin:@typescript-eslint/recommended',
    'plugin:react/recommended',
    'plugin:react-hooks/recommended',
    'plugin:jsx-a11y/recommended',
    'plugin:import/errors',

    'react-hooks/rules-of-hooks': 'error',
    'react-hooks/exhaustive-deps': 'warn',

    // Import
    'import/order': ['error', {
      'groups': [
        'builtin',

        'internal',
        'parent',
        'sibling',
        'index'
      ],
      'newlines-between': 'always',
      'alphabetize': { order: 'asc' }
    }],
    'import/no-unresolved': 'error',
    'import/named': 'error',

    // 通用
    'no-console': ['warn', { allow: ['warn', 'error'] }],

    'eqeqeq': ['error', 'always'],

  settings: {
    react: {
      version: 'detect'

    'import/resolver': {
      typescript: {}
    }
  },

  // 覆盖
  overrides: [
    {
      files: ['*.test.ts', '*.spec.ts'],
      env: {
        jest: true
      },
      rules: {
        '@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any': 'off'
      }
    }
  ]
};
```

```json
// .prettierrc
{
```

**四、Husky配置**

```bash
# 安装
npm install husky --save-dev
npx husky install
npx husky add .husky/pre-commit "npm run lint"
npx husky add .husky/commit-msg "npx commitlint --edit $1"
```

```json
// package.json
{
  "scripts": {
    "lint": "eslint src --ext .ts,.tsx",
    "lint:fix": "eslint src --ext .ts,.tsx --fix",
    "format": "prettier --write \"src/**/*.{ts,tsx,css,json}\"",
    "type-check": "tsc --noEmit",
    "prepare": "husky install"
  },
  "lint-staged": {
    "*.{ts,tsx}": [
      "eslint --fix",
      "prettier --write"
    ],
    "*.{css,scss}": [
      "prettier --write"
    ]
  }
}
```

**五、TypeScript配置**

```json
    "noFallthroughCasesInSwitch": true,
    "skipLibCheck": true,

    "paths": {
      "@/*": ["src/*"],
      "@components/*": ["src/components/*"],
      "@utils/*": ["src/utils/*"]
    }
  },
  "include": ["src"],
  "exclude": ["node_modules", "dist"]
}
```

### 20.3 CI/CD流程设计

**面试问题：如何设计前端CI/CD流程？**

**参考答案：**

**一、CI/CD流程架构**

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                      CI/CD流程架构                              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                                 │
│  代码提交 ──> 代码检查 ──> 构建 ──> 测试 ──> 部署                │
│     │            │           │       │       │                  │
│     ▼            ▼           ▼       ▼       ▼                  │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │                    CI 持续集成                           │   │
│  │  • 代码质量检查                                           │   │
│  │  • 单元测试                                              │   │
│  │  • 构建打包                                              │   │
│  │  • 集成测试                                              │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                           │                                    │
│                           ▼                                    │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│  │                    CD 持续部署                          │   │
│  │  • 预览环境                                              │   │
│  │  • 测试环境                                              │   │
│  │  • 生产环境                                              │   │
│  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│                                                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**二、GitHub Actions配置**

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

env:
  NODE_VERSION: '18'

jobs:
  lint:
    name: Lint
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
          cache: 'npm'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check

      - name: ESLint
        run: npm run lint

      - name: Prettier
        run: npm run format -- --check

  test:
    name: Test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
          cache: 'npm'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Run tests
        run: npm run test -- --coverage

      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          files: ./coverage/lcov.info
          flags: unittests

  build:
    name: Build
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
          cache: 'npm'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Build
        run: npm run build

      - name: Upload build artifacts
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v3
        with:
          name: dist
          path: dist
```

```yaml
# .github/workflows/cd.yml
name: CD

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  deploy-preview:
    name: Deploy Preview
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.event_name == 'pull_request'

    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Build
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v20
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_PROJECT_ID }}
          vercel-args: '--prod=false'

  deploy-production:
    name: Deploy Production
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' && github.event_name == 'push'

    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Build
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Server
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@v0.1.0
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.HOST }}
          username: ${{ secrets.USERNAME }}
          key: ${{ secrets.KEY }}
          script: |
            cd /var/www/app
            docker-compose pull
            docker-compose up -d
```

**三、GitLab CI配置**

```yaml
# .gitlab-ci.yml
stages:
  - lint
  - test
  - build
  - deploy

variables:
  NODE_VERSION: "18"

before_script:
  - npm ci --cache .npm --prefer-offline

lint:
  stage: lint
  image: node:${NODE_VERSION}
  script:
    - npm run type-check
    - npm run lint
  cache:
    key: ${CI_COMMIT_REF_SLUG}
    paths:
      - .npm/

test:
  stage: test
  image: node:${NODE_VERSION}
  script:
    - npm run test -- --coverage
  coverage: '/All files[^|]*\|[^|]*\s+([\d\.]+)/'
  artifacts:
    reports:
      junit: junit.xml
      coverage_report:
        coverage_format: cobertura
        path: coverage/cobertura-coverage.xml

build:
  stage: build
  image: node:${NODE_VERSION}
  script:
    - npm run build
  artifacts:
    paths:
      - dist/
    expire_in: 1 hour

deploy_staging:
  stage: deploy
  image: alpine:latest
  script:
    - apk add --no-cache openssh-client
    - eval $(ssh-agent -s)
    - echo "$SSH_PRIVATE_KEY" | tr -d '\r' | ssh-add -
    - mkdir -p ~/.ssh
    - chmod 700 ~/.ssh
    - ssh-keyscan $DEPLOY_HOST >> ~/.ssh/known_hosts
    - scp -r dist/* $DEPLOY_USER@$DEPLOY_HOST:/var/www/staging/
  environment:
    name: staging
    url: https://staging.example.com
  only:
    - develop

deploy_production:
  stage: deploy
  image: alpine:latest
  script:
    - apk add --no-cache openssh-client
    - eval $(ssh-agent -s)
    - echo "$SSH_PRIVATE_KEY" | tr -d '\r' | ssh-add -
    - mkdir -p ~/.ssh
    - chmod 700 ~/.ssh
    - ssh-keyscan $DEPLOY_HOST >> ~/.ssh/known_hosts
    - scp -r dist/* $DEPLOY_USER@$DEPLOY_HOST:/var/www/production/
  environment:
    name: production
    url: https://example.com
  only:
    - main
  when: manual
```
